ValueSet: List of Conditions / Comorbidity

Official URL: http://openhie.org/fhir/covid19-casereporting/ValueSet/vs-conditions-comorbidity Version: 0.1.0-test
Active as of 2022-09-16 Responsible: OpenHIE Realm: Computable Name: VSConditionsComorbidity

List of Conditions / Comorbidity

References

  • Covid19 Conditions or comorbidity

Logical Definition (CLD)

This value set includes codes based on the following rules:

  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 49601007 (Cardiovascular disorder)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 13645005 (Chronic obstructive lung disease)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 118940003 (Neurological disorder)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 77176002 (Smoker)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 46635009 (Diabetes mellitus type I)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 44054006 (Diabetes mellitus type II)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 73211009 (Diabetes mellitus)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 165816005 (HTLV-3 antibody positive)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 38341003 (High blood pressure)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 234532001 (Immunodeficiency disorder)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 76783007 (Chronic hepatitis)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 363346000 (Malignant tumor)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 709044004 (Chronic kidney disease)
  • Include codes from http://snomed.info/sct where concept is-a 56717001 (Tuberculosis)
  • Include all codes defined in http://openhie.org/fhir/covid19-casereporting/CodeSystem/cs-other

 

Expansion

This value set has >1000 codes in it. In order to keep the publication size manageable, only a selection (1000 codes) of the whole set of codes is shown

Explanation of the columns that may appear on this page:

Level A few code lists that FHIR defines are hierarchical - each code is assigned a level. In this scheme, some codes are under other codes, and imply that the code they are under also applies
System The source of the definition of the code (when the value set draws in codes defined elsewhere)
Code The code (used as the code in the resource instance)
Display The display (used in the display element of a Coding). If there is no display, implementers should not simply display the code, but map the concept into their application
Definition An explanation of the meaning of the concept
Comments Additional notes about how to use the code
